First, they hustle and get your prescription ready fast so you can pick it up in the drive thru in a timely manner after your doctor visit. Second, the staff is friendly, knowledgeable and efficient. Third, it's easy to re-new prescriptions over the phone. Fourth, the pharmacy may be small inside, but the selection of stuff they have on the shelves is very good.  Fifth, they have home delivery for medicines. I have not used this service, but think it's a good service for the local community.  I highly recommend Avalon Pharmacy in Yucca Valley.< /Review>

Our cans had become very smelly, sticky, and disgusting after 5 years of owning our home. We booked Canology service, and they arrived the next week, the day after our weekly garbage collection.  Service was performed quickly and thoroughly, and our cans were sparkly clean and smelled fresh after service.

The only downside is there is not an option to have a driver contact you on arrival or shortly before to bring out your cans - they must be left along the street. This was unfortunate for us as our cleaning didn't occur until early afternoon, and I had to go out several times in the morning to remove decidedly not-bagged debris passersby deposited into our cans while they were curbside, which Canology informs you will disqualify you for service and subject you to a fee.

Overall, it was a great service, and something we'll likely do annually to keep our cans cleaner and avoid build-up inside them.<//Review>

Pleasantly surprised! We had been to this site previously under prior ownership  ... it had been a typical 'greasy spoon.' Things have been elevated! Still a bucket load of comfort food on the menu but it's minus the 'greasy' part! We were here at Breakfast time while having our car serviced up the street (at The Auto Shop, a honest-to-goodness HONEST mechanic,  Al Davis). Greeting was very friendly.  Server Brian proved to be a pleasure. We decided to split the Chicken Fried Steak & eggs plate as we had heard that the portion sizes here were quite generous. Even though Brian brought us steak knives, they weren't necessary as we could cut through they protein with our forks. The biscuits & gravy were spot on and the home fries are a winner. Can't wait to try other menu items! We'll surely schedule our next car service accordingly!</Review>

<rate>4</rate>< review>
The outside could use an upgrade but it's not too much of a problem. The inside dining area is about the size of a living room but has a lot of character.  The servers were really friendly in a way that seemed genuine. As in they were happy to be polite rather than only doing it otherwise they might get fired or something. It took a while to get my order but it was worth it and I doubt the place is ever empty. It's a bit far from where I live but if I'm in town with friends id be more than willing to bring them too.
Just keep in mind that they may not take American Express cards. Idk why but that wasn't a problem for me.

Tldr;
Pros:
- Great food
- Great prices
- Great Service

Cons:
- A bit odd looking on the outside and could probably use some form of shading for those that have to wait
- if they raise enough space maybe they can expand the building a bit to seat more people< /review>
